namespace = cultural_influence_greek	
#(Something in Greek!)

province_event = { #Aegean Greek settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.1
	title = greek_reclamation.title
	desc = greek_reclamation.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root

	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		agaio_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = tourkiki }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = rhomaio_formed }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = aegean_split }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a	

		change_culture = greek
	}
}

province_event = { #Illyrion settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.2
	title = greek_reclamation.title
	desc = greek_reclamation.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		illyrion_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = illyrion }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = illyrion
	}
}

	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		graiko_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = griko }

			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag

			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		}

			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}

		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		pontic_greek_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { has_global_flag = rhomaio_formed }
		NOT = { culture = pontic_greek }

			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}

			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {

province_event = { #Armenian Assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.6
	title = greek_reclamation_1.title
	desc = greek_reclamation_1.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_global_flag = hellenic_armenian_assimilation_flag
			owner = { primary_culture = nkreko_armenio }
		}	
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		nkreko_armenio_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = nkreko_armenio }
		ci_assimilation_check = yes
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { #Generic Assimilation MTTH
		years = 25

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			culture_group = byzantine
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			culture = armenian
		}

		#Dev. factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { development = 20 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 40
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}
		modifier = { #This is now some 80 years, don't see much reason to increment further
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}

		#Religion
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 0 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			religion_group = OWNER
		}

		#Misc
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			unrest = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_building = university
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			has_colonist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_capital_area = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation_1.a

		change_culture = nkreko_armenio
	}
}

province_event = { #Alexandrian settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.7
	title = greek_reclamation_2.title
	desc = greek_reclamation_2.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		alexandrian_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = alexandrian }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation_2.a

		change_culture = alexandrian
	}
}

			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		name = greek_conquest.d

		change_culture = varangian
	}
}

province_event = { #Avissinos settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.12
	title = greek_conquest_3.title
	desc = greek_conquest_3.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		avissinos_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = avissinos }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}	

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_conquest.e

		change_culture = avissinos
	}
}

country_event = { #Rhomaio merge
	id = cultural_influence_greek.15
	title = rhomaio_merger.title
	desc = rhomaio_merger.desc
	picture = GREAT_BUILDING_eventPicture

	major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			merge_rhomaio = yes
			set_global_flag = rhomaio_formed
		}
	}

	option = { #Constantinople
		name = rhomaio_merger.a	

		trigger = {
			owns = 151 #Constantinople
		}

		151 = { #Add College to Constantinople
			add_building = university
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = rhomaio_academy
				duration = -1
			}
			add_base_tax = 4
			add_base_production = 2
			add_base_manpower = 2
		}
	}

	option = { #Thessalonike
		name = rhomaio_merger.b

		trigger = {
			owns = 148 #Thessalonike
		}

		148 = { #Add College to Thessalonike
			add_building = university
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = rhomaio_academy
				duration = -1
			}
			add_base_tax = 4
			add_base_production = 2
			add_base_manpower = 2
		}
	}

	option = { #Athens

		trigger = {
			owns = 146 #Athens
		}

		146 = { #Add College to Athens

				duration = -1

	option = { #Arta
		name = rhomaio_merger.d

		trigger = {
			owns = 7131 #Arta
		}

		7131 = { #Add College to Arta, capital of the (Komnenos Doukas) Despotate of Epirus
			add_building = university
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = rhomaio_academy
				duration = -1
			}
			add_base_tax = 4
			add_base_production = 2
			add_base_manpower = 2
		}
	}

	option = { #Nikaia
		name = rhomaio_merger.e

		trigger = {
			owns = 5157 #Nikaia
		}

		5157 = { #Add College to Nikaia
			add_building = university
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = rhomaio_academy
				duration = -1
			}

			add_base_production = 2
			add_base_manpower = 2
		}
	}
	option = { #Trebizond
		name = rhomaio_merger.f

			owns = 330 #Trebizond
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation_2.a

		change_culture = kirenike
	}
}

province_event = { #Carthaginian settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.18
	title = greek_conquest_5.title
	desc = greek_conquest_5.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		karchidoniac_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = karchidoniac }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_conquest.h

		change_culture = karchidoniac
	}
}

		change_culture = indiki_koilada
	}
}

province_event = { #Massalian settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.23
	title = greek_conquest_9.title
	desc = greek_conquest_9.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		massalian_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = massalian }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = massalian
	}
}

		italiote_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = italiote }
		ci_settlement_check = yes

			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)

		}

			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {

			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors

			factor = 3

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = velgoi
	}
}

province_event = { #Pannonion settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.29
	title = greek_conquest_13.title
	desc = greek_conquest_13.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		pannonion_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = pannonion }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = pannonion
	}
}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = notioanatolikos_germanikos
	}
}

province_event = { #Northeastern Germania settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.34
	title = greek_conquest_15.title
	desc = greek_conquest_15.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		voreioanatolikosgermanikos_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = voreioanatolikos_germanikos }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = voreioanatolikos_germanikos
	}
}

province_event = { #Makria Savramata settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.39
	title = greek_conquest_17.title
	desc = greek_conquest_17.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		makria_savramata_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = makria_savramata }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = makria_savramata
	}
}

		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = kavlika
	}
}

province_event = { #Thivetiani settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.45
	title = greek_conquest_22.title
	desc = greek_conquest_22.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		thivetiani_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = thivetiani }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = thivetiani
	}
}

			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {

			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}

province_event = { #Koniaka settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.50
	title = greek_conquest_24.title
	desc = greek_conquest_24.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		koniaka_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = koniaka }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = koniaka
	}
}

		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		polinesika_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = polinesika }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = polinesika
	}
}

province_event = { #Erimos Aethiopas settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.56
	title = greek_conquest_africa.title
	desc = greek_conquest_africa.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		erimos_aethiopas_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = erimos_aethiopas }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_conquest_africa.a

		change_culture = erimos_aethiopas
	}
}

		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_conquest_africa.a

		change_culture = souachiliaktikos
	}
}

province_event = { #Olissoponion settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.61
	title = greek_conquest_11.title
	desc = greek_conquest_11.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		olissiponion_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = olissiponion }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = olissiponion
	}
}

province_event = { #Turkish assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.62
	title = greek_conquest_28.title
	desc = greek_conquest_28.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		culture = turkish
		has_global_flag = hellenic_turkish_assimilation_flag
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		NOT = { culture = tourkiki }
		ci_assimilation_check = yes
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}	

	mean_time_to_happen = { #Generic Assimilation MTTH
		years = 25

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Dev. factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { development = 20 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 40
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}
		modifier = { #This is now some 80 years, don't see much reason to increment further
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}

		#Religion
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 0 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			religion_group = OWNER
		}

		#Misc
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			unrest = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_building = university
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			has_colonist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_capital_area = no
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a

		change_culture = tourkiki
	}
}

	id = cultural_influence_greek.66
	title = greek_reclamation.title
	desc = greek_reclamation.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root

	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		cypriot_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = cypriot }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = rhomaio_formed }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a	

		change_culture = cypriot
	}
}

country_event = { #Aegean merge
	id = cultural_influence_greek.67
	title = aegean_merger.title
	desc = aegean_merger.desc
	picture = GREAT_BUILDING_eventPicture

	major = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			merge_aegean = yes
			clr_global_flag = aegean_split
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = aegean_merger.a	#No special bonus, that goes to the big merge
	}
}

country_event = { #Aegean split
	id = cultural_influence_greek.69
	title = aegean_split.title
	desc = aegean_split.desc
	picture = CITY_VIEW_eventPicture

	major = yes

	trigger = {
		is_year = 1475 #Delay until 1475 
		any_owned_province = { #Make sure it actually fires for someone relevant
			culture = greek
		}
		AND = {
			GRE = { exists = no } #Greece and Byzantium musn't exist, this expects the BR event to turn Byzantium into Morea
			BYZ = { exists = no }
		}	
		OR = {
			AND = { #Provinces fell to Foreign rule
				calc_true_if = {
					all_province = {
						culture = greek
						owner = { NOT = { primary_culture = greek } }
					}
					amount = 25
				}
			}
			151 = { #Constantinople is under foreign control (Principally checking for Ottomans, but anyone counts)
				OWNER = {
					NOT = { culture_group = byzantine }
				}
			}
			exists = LTE #Latin Empire has formed
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
		NOT = { has_global_flag = aegean_split }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			exists = MOE #Morea
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			split_aegean = yes
			set_global_flag = aegean_split
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					primary_culture = greek
				}
				country_event = {
					id = cultural_influence_greek.70 #Pick new Primary
					days = 0
				}
			}			
		}
	}

	option = { 
		name = aegean_split.a	
	}
}

	picture = CITY_VIEW_eventPicture

		is_year = 1500 #Delay until 1500 (if you somehow manage to actually unite these and then lose 50 provinces before 1500 I would be surprised)

			culture = anatolikos
		}
		OR = {
			AND = { #Provinces fell to Foreign rule

				}
			}
		}

		has_global_flag = anatolian_merge
	}

		years = 50

			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag

	}
