province_event = { #Thracian settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.75
	title = greek_reclamation.title
	desc = greek_reclamation.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root

	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		thracian_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = hellenic_thracian }
		NOT = { culture = hellas_culture }
		has_global_flag = aegean_split
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { has_country_modifier = greco_armenian_theory_modifier }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a	

		change_culture = hellenic_thracian
	}
}

province_event = { #Macedonian settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.76
	title = greek_reclamation.title
	desc = greek_reclamation.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root

	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		macedonian_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = macedonian }
		NOT = { culture = hellas_culture }
		has_global_flag = aegean_split
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { has_country_modifier = greco_armenian_theory_modifier }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a	

		change_culture = macedonian
	}
}

	id = cultural_influence_greek.77

			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag

			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)

			has_terrain = glacier
		}

			}	
		}

			factor = 1.5
			OR = {

				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8

		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)

			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation.a	

		change_culture = epirotan
	}
}

			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag

		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2

		}

			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {

province_event = { #Expansion of Hellas Culture under foreign rule, comes to replace other Greek dialects in the Aegean to become what we now know as Modern Greek
	id = cultural_influence_greek.81
	title = greek_hellas_foreign.title
	desc = greek_hellas_foreign.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root

	trigger = {
		owner = { NOT = { culture_group = byzantine } } #Foreign rule only
		owner = { accepted_culture = hellas_culture }
		agaio_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = hellas_culture }
		OR = {
			NOT = { culture_group = OWNER } #Don't want this spreading to Turkish provinces as the Ottomans for example, Phanariot Greeks event in the Turkish file already does that anyway to a minor extent (which can be ignored anyway)
			culture_group = byzantine #Permit any Greeks to merge, incase AI accepts other greek splinter cultures
			AND = {
				has_owner_accepted_culture = no #Or accepted Bulgarians
				NOT = { culture_group = byzantine } #Except other Greeks
			}	
		}	
		OR = { #Influence check
			any_neighbor_province = { culture = hellas_culture }
			any_friendly_coast_border_province = { culture = hellas_culture }
			has_building = university
			province_trade_power = 15
			development = 30
		}
		has_global_flag = aegean_split #If reunification occurs this makes no sense
		printing_press = 100 #Check if province has institution not country
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
		NOT = { has_province_modifier = hellas_culture_settlers_scorned } #Previously prevented, however attempts to settle will continue causing further unrest after the modifier wears off and they are prevented again
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { #Generic Assimilation MTTH
		years = 25

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			culture_group = byzantine
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OWNER = { has_country_modifier = greco_armenian_theory_modifier }
		}

		#Dev. factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			NOT = { development = 20 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 40
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}
		modifier = { #This is now some 80 years, don't see much reason to increment further
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
			NOT = { has_building = university }
		}

		#Religion
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			NOT = { tolerance_to_this = 0 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			religion_group = OWNER
		}

		#Misc
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			unrest = 1
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_building = university
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			has_colonist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_capital_area = no
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_hellas_foreign.a
		
		change_culture = hellas_culture
	}
	option = {
		name = greek_hellas_foreign.b	#Preserve the local inhabitants (only available to non Hellenic provinces, such as Arvanites)
		
		trigger = {
			NOT = { culture_group = byzantine }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = "hellas_culture_settlers_scorned"
			duration = 7300 #20 Years
		}
	}	
}


province_event = { #Mesopotamian settlements and assimilation
	id = cultural_influence_greek.82
	title = greek_reclamation_2.title
	desc = greek_reclamation_2.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		hellenic_mesopotamian_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = hellenic_mesopotamian }
		ci_settlement_check = yes
		OR = { #Players can do it before the decision provided they dev it, or send a colonist. Due to Byzantium's Exarchs AIs are allowed to do it if their overlord (presumably the player) has it.
			owner = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements }
			owner = { ai = no }
			AND = {
				owner = { overlord = { has_country_modifier = hellenic_settlements } }
				ai = yes
			}	
		}
		has_global_flag = CI_events_enabled
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 20

		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}

		#Terrain factors (These replace pre-0.6.1 low dev penalties, which were simulating the same thing) (This was basically done to better simulate the German settlements in Banat)
		#Farmlands & Grasslands are ideal and act as the base 1.0 modifier (Marsh is also treated as Grasslands since it is difficult to tell if the Marsh has been drained)
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_terrain = glacier
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_terrain = mountain
				has_terrain = desert
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_terrain = highlands
				has_terrain = hills
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = { 
				has_terrain = woods
				has_terrain = drylands
			}	
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_terrain = forest
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.8
			has_terrain = coastal_desert
		}
		#Climatic factors (Tropical ignored, as it isn't universally difficult to settle, only for the Temperate peoples)
		modifier = {
			has_climate = arid
			factor = 2
		}

		#Dev button factors
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 5
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			num_of_times_improved_by_owner = 10
		}

		#Dev Factors, penalties begin at 30 Dev
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 30
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			development = 40
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 50
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 60
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			development = 70
		}

		#Misc factors
		modifier = { #Passive settlement (I.E without a colonist)
			factor = 3
			has_colonist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.4
			has_owner_religion = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			owner = { adm = 6 }
		}
		#modifier = { #Don't like this, since misc got merged into BT adm focus will be active most of the time now for the advisor cost
		#	factor = 0.75
		#	national_focus = adm
		#}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_reclamation_2.a

		change_culture = hellenic_mesopotamian
	}
}

#Colonial Cultures

namespace = cultural_influence_greek_colonial
#(Another something in greek!)

province_event = { #Boreaka Colonial Settlement event
	id = cultural_influence_greek_colonial.1
	title = greco_voreaka_settlement.title
	desc = greco_voreaka_settlement.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		voreaka_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = voreaka }
		is_city = yes
		OWNER = { culture_group = byzantine }
		any_neighbor_province = { culture_group = byzantine }		
		ci_colonial_settlement_check = yes
		has_global_flag = greco_voreaka_established_flag
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50	#50 years for native cultures to get settled
		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {	#About 15 years for colonies to diverge (this is after the initial establishment which results in about 85 years total for the earlier provinces)
			factor = 0.30
			hellenic_old_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.15	#About 7.5 years if a separate colonial culture
			hellenic_new_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {	#Once the first provinces flip neighbours will flip faster
			factor = 0.5
			any_neighbor_province = { culture = voreaka }
		}
		modifier = {	#If independence is achieved divergence is quicker
			factor = 0.4
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				owner = { is_former_colonial_nation = yes }
			}	
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = byzantine
					capital_scope = { #This is a fallback trigger in case any new tags spawn after the initial establishment event
						voreaka_culture_region = yes
					}
				}
				change_primary_culture = voreaka 
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = greco_voreaka_settlement.a

		change_culture = voreaka
		if = {
			limit = { OWNER = { NOT = { accepted_culture = voreaka } } }
			add_accepted_culture = voreaka
		}			#Adding culture as an accepted culture to prevent AI flipping, and to not penalise player in a no-choice culture event		
	}
}

		modifier = {	#Once the first provinces flip neighbours will flip faster
			factor = 0.5
			any_neighbor_province = { culture = kentrika }
		}
		modifier = {	#If independence is achieved divergence is quicker
			factor = 0.4
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				owner = { is_former_colonial_nation = yes }
			}	
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = byzantine
					capital_scope = { #This is a fallback trigger in case any new tags spawn after the initial establishment event
						kentrika_culture_region = yes
					}
				}
				change_primary_culture = kentrika 
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = greco_kentrika_settlement.a

		change_culture = kentrika
		if = {
			limit = { OWNER = { NOT = { accepted_culture = kentrika } } }
			add_accepted_culture = kentrika
		}			#Adding culture as an accepted culture to prevent AI flipping, and to not penalise player in a no-choice culture event		
	}
}

province_event = { #Dyitinisika Colonial settlement event
	id = cultural_influence_greek_colonial.6
	title = greco_dyitinisika_settlement.title
	desc = greco_dyitinisika_settlement.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root

		dyitinisika_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = dyitinisika }
		is_city = yes
		OWNER = { culture_group = byzantine }
		any_neighbor_province = { culture_group = byzantine }		
		ci_colonial_settlement_check = yes
		has_global_flag = greco_dyitinisika_established_flag
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50	#50 years for native cultures to get settled
		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {	#About 15 years for colonies to diverge (this is after the initial establishment which results in about 85 years total for the earlier provinces)
			factor = 0.30
			hellenic_old_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.15	#About 7.5 years if a separate colonial culture
			hellenic_new_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {	#Once the first provinces flip neighbours will flip faster
			factor = 0.5
			any_neighbor_province = { culture = dyitinisika }

country_event = { #Establishment of Boreaka
	id = cultural_influence_greek_colonial.13
	title = greco_voreaka_establishment.title
	desc = greco_voreaka_establishment.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		any_owned_province = {
			AND = {
				voreaka_culture_region = yes
				culture_group = byzantine
			}	
		}
		culture_group = byzantine
		NOT = { has_global_flag = greco_voreaka_established_flag }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 70
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = greco_voreaka_established_flag
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = byzantine
					capital_scope = { voreaka_culture_region = yes }
				}
				capital_scope = { change_culture = voreaka }
				change_primary_culture = voreaka
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = greco_voreaka_establishment.a
		custom_tooltip = greco_voreaka_established_convert_tags
	}
}

				culture_group = byzantine
			}	
		}
		culture_group = byzantine
		NOT = { has_global_flag = greco_dytiaktika_established_flag }
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 70
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = greco_dytiaktika_established_flag
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = byzantine
					capital_scope = { dytiaktika_culture_region = yes }
				}
				capital_scope = { change_culture = dytiaktika }
				change_primary_culture = dytiaktika
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = greco_dytiaktika_establishment.a
		custom_tooltip = greco_dytiaktika_established_convert_tags
	}
}

province_event = { #Settlement of the Frontier
	id = cultural_influence_greek_colonial.25
	title = greek_colony.title
	desc = greek_colony.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			native_american_trigger = yes #Native cultures
			is_capital = yes
		}	
		owner = { culture_group = byzantine }
		hellenic_old_worlder_country = yes	#Once the colonial language is established they will use their own events instead, if it's a crown colony then either event can fire, eventually it will flip to the colonial varient
		ci_colonial_settlement_check = yes
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		#Template Settled MTTH
		years = 50

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			owner = { has_idea_to_settle_faster = yes }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				owner = { is_colonial_nation = yes }
				owner = { is_former_colonial_nation = yes }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			any_neighbor_province = {
				culture = OWNER
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			religion = OWNER
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			is_capital = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = greek_colony.a

		change_culture = OWNER
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { religion_group = OWNER }
			}
			change_religion = OWNER
		}	
	}
}

province_event = { #Arktiks Colonial settlement event
	id = cultural_influence_greek_colonial.31
	title = greco_arctic_settlement.title
	desc = greco_arctic_settlement.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		greco_arctic_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = greco_arctic_culture }
		is_city = yes
		OWNER = { culture_group = byzantine }
		any_neighbor_province = { culture_group = byzantine }		
		ci_colonial_settlement_check = yes
		has_global_flag = greco_arctic_established_flag
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50	#50 years for native cultures to get settled
		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {	#About 15 years for colonies to diverge (this is after the initial establishment which results in about 85 years total for the earlier provinces)
			factor = 0.30
			hellenic_old_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.15	#About 7.5 years if a separate colonial culture
			hellenic_new_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {	#Once the first provinces flip neighbours will flip faster
			factor = 0.5
			any_neighbor_province = { culture = greco_arctic_culture }
		}
		modifier = {	#If independence is achieved divergence is quicker
			factor = 0.4
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				owner = { is_former_colonial_nation = yes }
			}	
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = byzantine
					capital_scope = { #This is a fallback trigger in case any new tags spawn after the initial establishment event
						greco_arctic_culture_region = yes
					}
				}
				change_primary_culture = greco_arctic_culture 
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = greco_arctic_settlement.a

		change_culture = greco_arctic_culture
		if = {
			limit = { OWNER = { NOT = { accepted_culture = greco_arctic_culture } } }
			add_accepted_culture = greco_arctic_culture
		}			#Adding culture as an accepted culture to prevent AI flipping, and to not penalise player in a no-choice culture event		
	}
}

province_event = { #Limmnika Colonial settlement event
	id = cultural_influence_greek_colonial.33
	title = greco_limmnika_settlement.title
	desc = greco_limmnika_settlement.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		limnika_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = limmnika }
		is_city = yes
		OWNER = { culture_group = byzantine }
		any_neighbor_province = { culture_group = byzantine }		
		ci_colonial_settlement_check = yes
		has_global_flag = greco_limmnika_established_flag
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50	#50 years for native cultures to get settled
		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {	#About 15 years for colonies to diverge (this is after the initial establishment which results in about 85 years total for the earlier provinces)
			factor = 0.30
			hellenic_old_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.15	#About 7.5 years if a separate colonial culture
			hellenic_new_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {	#Once the first provinces flip neighbours will flip faster
			factor = 0.5
			any_neighbor_province = { culture = limmnika }
		}
		modifier = {	#If independence is achieved divergence is quicker
			factor = 0.4
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				owner = { is_former_colonial_nation = yes }
			}	
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					culture_group = byzantine
					capital_scope = { #This is a fallback trigger in case any new tags spawn after the initial establishment event
						limnika_culture_region = yes
					}
				}
				change_primary_culture = limmnika 
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = greco_limmnika_settlement.a

		change_culture = limmnika
		if = {
			limit = { OWNER = { NOT = { accepted_culture = limmnika } } }
			add_accepted_culture = limmnika
		}			#Adding culture as an accepted culture to prevent AI flipping, and to not penalise player in a no-choice culture event		
	}
}

province_event = { #Argentins Colonial settlement event
	id = cultural_influence_greek_colonial.34
	title = greco_argentine_settlement.title
	desc = greco_argentine_settlement.desc
	picture = CULTURE_eventPicture
	goto = root
	
	trigger = {
		greco_argentine_culture_region = yes
		NOT = { culture = greco_argentine_culture }
		is_city = yes
		OWNER = { culture_group = byzantine }
		any_neighbor_province = { culture_group = byzantine }		
		ci_colonial_settlement_check = yes
		has_global_flag = greco_argentine_established_flag
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 50	#50 years for native cultures to get settled
		#MTTH settings
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.0
			has_global_flag = 00_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_global_flag = 05_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_global_flag = 15_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.0
			has_global_flag = 20_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4.0
			has_global_flag = 40_CI_MTTH_flag
		}
		modifier = {	#About 15 years for colonies to diverge (this is after the initial establishment which results in about 85 years total for the earlier provinces)
			factor = 0.30
			hellenic_old_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.15	#About 7.5 years if a separate colonial culture
			hellenic_new_worlder = yes
		}
		modifier = {	#Once the first provinces flip neighbours will flip faster
			factor = 0.5
			any_neighbor_province = { culture = greco_argentine_culture }
		}
		modifier = {	#If independence is achieved divergence is quicker
			factor = 0.4
			AND = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				owner = { is_former_colonial_nation = yes }
			}

					}
				}
				change_primary_culture = greco_argentine_culture 
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = greco_argentine_settlement.a

		change_culture = greco_argentine_culture
		if = {
			limit = { OWNER = { NOT = { accepted_culture = greco_argentine_culture } } }
			add_accepted_culture = greco_argentine_culture
		}			#Adding culture as an accepted culture to prevent AI flipping, and to not penalise player in a no-choice culture event		
	}
}
